interop bridge consists of several interconnected layers:\\n\\n## Entry Point Detection and Main Execution\\n\\nThe entry point for ESM/CJS module loading detection begins in `lib/internal/modules/run_main.js`. The `executeUserEntryPoint()` function determines whether to use the ESM loader based on file extensions (.mjs), package.json type field, or explicit --experimental-default-type flag. The `runEntryPointWithESMLoader()` function initializes the ESM loader and executes user imports before running the entry point, with `asyncRunEntryPointWithESMLoader()` handling the actual async execution.\\n\\n## ModuleLoader Class and Core Loader\\n\\nThe central component is the `ModuleLoader` class in `lib/internal/modules/esm/loader.js` (lines 110+). This class manages:\\n- Resolution cache (#resolveCache) using ResolveCache from module_map.js\\n- Load cache (loadCache) using LoadCache from module_map.js  \\n- Module translators using translators from translators.js\\n- Customizations for loader hooks\\n- Import metadata initialization\\n- Module resolution and loading through the resolve/load/translate pipeline\\n\\nThe `createModuleLoader()` function (lines 801+) instantiates the loader, and `getOrInitializeCascadedLoader()` provides a singleton instance for cascaded loader chain support.\\n\\n## Module Job Pipeline and Linking\\n\\n`ModuleJob` class in `lib/internal/modules/esm/module_job.js` (lines 72+) represents a single module's loading state with:\\n- ModuleWrap binding from the C++ module\\n- Module promise for async compilation\\n- Linking pipeline (_link method, line 100+) that processes dependencies\\n- Evaluation pipeline (_evaluate method) for executing module code\\n- Support for both source text modules and synthetic modules\\n\\nThe linking phase connects all module dependencies recursively before evaluation.\\n\\n## Module Resolution\\n\\n`lib/internal/modules/esm/resolve.js` contains the resolution algorithm:\\n- `defaultResolve()` function performs standard module specifier resolution\\n- Package.json exports/imports resolution using `packageExportsResolve()` and `packageImportsResolve()`\\n- URL-based resolution for file://, data:, and node: protocol URLs\\n- Import attributes (formerly assertions) validation\\n- Specifier normalization and package boundary detection\\n\\n## CJS-ESM Interop Bridge\\n\\n`lib/internal/modules/cjs/loader.js` implements the ESM fallback for CommonJS:\\n- `finalizeEsmResolution()` function (line 1258) bridges CJS module loading with ESM resolution\\n- Uses packageExportsResolve and packageImportsResolve from esm/resolve.js for package exports in CommonJS context\\n- Enables require() in CommonJS modules to resolve ESM package exports\\n- CJS loader integration at module._compile() for ESM-compatible module loading\\n\\n## Module Format Detection and Translation\\n\\n`lib/internal/modules/esm/get_format.js` provides format detection:\\n- `defaultGetFormat()` function (line 240+) determines module format from file extension and content\\n- Supports 'module', 'commonjs', 'json', 'wasm', and 'builtin' formats\\n- Handles .mjs, .cjs, .js, .json file extensions with package.json type field support\\n\\n`lib/internal/modules/esm/formats.js` defines format metadata:\\n- Extension to format mapping (extensionFormatMap)\\n- MIME type to format mapping (mimeToFormat)\\n- Format validation for import attributes\\n- Wasm module support detection\\n\\n`lib/internal/modules/esm/translators.js` (lines 97+) translates modules into ModuleWrap objects:\\n- 'module' translator for JavaScript ES modules (line 97)\\n- 'commonjs' translator for CJS modules using cjs-module-lexer\\n- 'json' translator for JSON files\\n- 'wasm' translator for WebAssembly modules\\n- 'builtin' translator for Node.js built-in modules\\n- Each translator produces a ModuleWrap via ModuleJob\\n\\n## Module Loading Pipeline\\n\\n`lib/internal/modules/esm/load.js` implements the load hook:\\n- `defaultLoad()` function (line 87) fetches source code\\n- `getSource()` async function for file:// and data: protocol
